<script>
    (function() {

        (function() {
            if (!window.meta || !window.meta.requestTime) return;

            var initialClientTime = new Date().getTime();
            var reqElapsed;

            if (window.enablePerformance) {
                var timing = window.performance.timing;
                reqElapsed = initialClientTime - timing.requestStart;
            }
            else {
                //guess how long it took
                reqElapsed = 500;
            }

            var initialLogTime = window.meta.requestTime + reqElapsed;

            window.logOffset = initialLogTime - initialClientTime;
        })();

        window.beaconQueue = [];

        window.beacon = function(level, events, payload, force, synchronous) {

            // Set up payload

            payload = payload || {};

            payload.event = events.join('|');
            payload.state = 'pre_bootstrap';
            payload.level = level;
            payload.token = 'EC-0AL30315245124141';
            payload.pageID = window.meta && window.meta.pageID;
            payload.timestamp = window.logOffset ?
                new Date(window.logOffset + Date.now()).toString() :
                new Date();

            if (window.enablePerformance) {
                var performance = window.performance;
                var timing      = window.performance.timing || {};

                if (window.clientStartTime) {
                    payload.client_elapsed = parseInt(performance.now() - window.clientStartTime);
                }

                if (timing.connectEnd && timing.navigationStart) {
                    payload.req_elapsed = parseInt(performance.now() - (timing.connectEnd - timing.navigationStart));
                }
            }

            if (!force && level !== 'error' && level !== 'warn') {
                return beaconQueue.push(payload);
            }


            if (window.console && window.console.log) {
                console.log(payload.event, payload);
            }

            // Build URL

            var url   = 'https://www.sandbox.paypal.com/xoplatform/logger/api/log?';
            var query = [];

            for (var prop in payload) {
                query.push(encodeURIComponent(prop) + '=' + encodeURIComponent(payload[prop]));
            }

            url += query.join('&');

            // Set up request
            var req = new XMLHttpRequest();
            req.open('GET', url, !Boolean(synchronous));
            req.send(null);
        };

        window.fallback = function(reason, payload) {
            // Redirect to the error page
            function redirectToError() {
                return window.location = '/webapps/hermes/error';
            }

            // Fallback whitelist experiment: if error reason is not in the whitelist and passes the throttle, go to error page instead
            if (
                10 &&
                !~('windowload_timed_out,bootstrap_failed,buyer_ineligible,transaction_ineligible,ui_unhandled_response_status_404,ul_load_timeout,ui_unhandled_api_error,gce_not_supported,UNSUPPORTED_CUP_SECURECARD,INVALID_IBAN_CODE,MANDATE_METHOD_NOT_ELIGIBLE,SEPA_ACCEPT_CONTINGENCY,ROUTING_NUMBER_NOT_SUPPORTED,fallback_merchant_BA_nocards'.split(',')).indexOf(reason)
            ) {
                if ((Math.random() * 100) < 10) {
                    window.beacon('error', ['fallback_reason_not_whitelisted_treatment'], {reason: reason});

                    return redirectToError();
                } else {
                    window.beacon('error', ['fallback_reason_not_whitelisted_control'], {reason: reason});
                }
            }

            // Determine if we need to make an exception to the fallbacks based on the merchant ID, or as an alternative the country
                var exceptions = {
    "K5GPWSS6GRSTC": [
        "windowload_timed_out"
    ],
    "H2TCH5BL3VBH4": [
        "windowload_timed_out"
    ],
    "BR": [
        "windowload_timed_out"
    ]
};
                var country = 'US';
                var merchantId = 'VSF5E2W5RFWVU';
                var isMobile = ;

                // If we have a valid merchant Id
                if (merchantId.length > 1) {
                    // and merchant Id is in the exceptions list
                    if (exceptions[merchantId]) {
                        if (exceptions[merchantId].indexOf(reason) === -1) {
                            window.beacon('error', ['fallback_to_error_page'], {reason: reason});
                            return redirectToError();
                        }

                        window.beacon('error', ['fallback_ignored'], {reason: reason});
                        return;
                    }
                } else {
                    // If it's a mobile device and the country is in the exceptions list
                    if (isMobile && exceptions[country]) {

                        if (exceptions[country].indexOf(reason) === -1) {
                            window.beacon('error', ['fallback_to_error_page'], {reason: reason});
                            return redirectToError();
                        }

                        window.beacon('error', ['fallback_ignored'], {reason: reason});
                        return;
                    }
                }

            window.fallback = function() {};

            payload = payload || {};
            payload.reason = reason;

            window.beacon('error', [reason, 'fallback', 'fallback_reason_' + reason], payload);

            setTimeout(function() {
                if (~window.location.hostname.indexOf('localhost')) {
                    return console.log('Fallback inhibited on localhost');
                }

                window.onbeforeunload = function() {};
                window.location = '' + meta.fallbackURL + '&token=EC-0AL30315245124141&fallback=1&reason=' + reason;
            }, 500);
        };

        function isPaymentRequestAPISupported() {
            var currentVersionMatch = navigator.userAgent.match(/Chrome\/([0-9]+)\./i);
            return window.navigator.vendor === 'Google Inc.'
                    && 'PaymentRequest' in window
                    && navigator.userAgent.match(/Android/i)
                    && currentVersionMatch
                    && Number(currentVersionMatch[1]) >= 58;
        }

        // Create PaymentRequest object
        function createPaymentRequest() {
            var supportedInstruments = [
                {
                    supportedMethods: ['https://android.com/pay'],
                    data: {
                        minGooglePlayServicesVersion: '10400000',
                        paymentMethodTokenizationParameters: {
                            tokenizationType: 'GATEWAY_TOKEN',
                            parameters: {
                                gateway: 'paypal'
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            ];
            var details = {
                // Payment request requires an amount. Hardcode the value for now.
                total: {label: 'Checkout', amount: {currency: 'USD', value: '1.00'}}
            };

            var options = {};
            return new PaymentRequest(supportedInstruments, details, options);  // eslint-disable-line no-undef
        }

        if (isPaymentRequestAPISupported()) {
            try {
                window.appPaymentRequest = createPaymentRequest();
            } catch(e) {
                window.beacon('error', ['create_payment_request_error'], {
                    name: e && e.name,
                    msg: e && e.message
                });
            }
        }

        // Experimental setting for window load timeout.
        var wl_throttle = 50;
        var wl_testTimeout = 50000;
        var timeout = (Math.floor(Math.random() * 100) < wl_throttle) ? wl_testTimeout : 20000;
        window.beacon('info', ['windowload_timeout_setting'], {'timeout': timeout, 'throttle': wl_throttle}, true);
        var windowLoadTimeout = setTimeout(function() {
            if (!window.bootstrap) {
                return window.fallback('windowload_timed_out');
            }
        }, timeout);

        window.onload = function() {
            clearTimeout(windowLoadTimeout);
        };

        // Log beforeunload event to track of number of users leaving the page before app gets loaded.
        window.onbeforeunload = function() {
            clearTimeout(windowLoadTimeout);
            window.beacon('info', ['pre_bootstrap_window_beforeunload'], {'timeout': timeout, 'throttle': wl_throttle},
                    true, true);
        };

        var windowErrorCache = [];

        window.onerror = function(message, file, line, col, err) {
            message = message && (message.stack || message).toString();

            if (!~windowErrorCache.indexOf(message)) {
                windowErrorCache.push(message);
                beacon('error', ['pre_window_error'], {
                    message: message,
                    file: file && file.toString(),
                    line: line && line.toString(),
                    col: col && col.toString(),
                    stack: err && (err.stack || err).toString()
                });
            }
        };

        window.scripterror = function(event) {
            window.beacon('error', ['script_error'], {
                script: event.target.attributes.src.value
            });
        };

        window.beacon('info', ['pre_bootstrap']);

    })();
</script>

<script>
    (function() {
        var tealeaf;
        // start dynamic script insertion as soon as possible
            tealeaf = {
    "throttle": "5",
    "captureMode": "domcap",
    "scriptSrcPattern": "https://www.paypalobjects.com/js/xo/tealeaf-hermes-prod-02_%.min.js"
};
        if (!tealeaf) {
            return;
        }

        var domcap = 'domcap', classic = 'classic';

        var throttleValue;

        var override = getOverride();
        if (override) {
            window.beacon('info', ['tealeaf_override']);
            throttleValue = -Infinity;
            tealeaf.captureMode = override;
        }
        else {
            throttleValue = hashStr(window.meta.token) % 100;
        }


        if (tealeaf.captureMode !== domcap && tealeaf.captureMode !== classic) {
            window.beacon('info', ['tealeaf_not_enabled'], { reason: 'not_configured' });
            return;
        }

        if (!tealeaf.throttle || throttleValue > parseInt(tealeaf.throttle)) {
            window.beacon('info', ['tealeaf_not_enabled'], { reason: 'throttle' });
            return;
        }

        try {
            var captureMode = tealeaf.captureMode === domcap && validBrowser() ?
                domcap : classic;

            window.beacon('info', ['tealeaf_enabled'], { captureMode: captureMode });

            var script = document.createElement('script');
            script.src = getSrc(captureMode);
            // block execution but not parsing
            // tealeaf needs to be included before 'onload' happens
            script.async = false;
            script.onerror = window.scripterror;
            document.head.appendChild(script);
        }
        catch (e) {
            window.beacon('error', ['tealeaf_include_failed'], {
                name: e && e.name,
                msg: e && e.message
            });
        }

        function getOverride() {
            if (window.location.search.indexOf('tealeaf_domcap_override') !== -1) return domcap;
            if (window.location.search.indexOf('tealeaf_classic_override') !== -1) return classic;
        }

        function getSrc(captureMode) {
            return tealeaf.scriptSrcPattern.replace('%', captureMode);
        }

        function validBrowser() {
            var ieVersion = new Function("/*@cc_on return @_jscript_version; @*/")();

            if (!ieVersion) return true;

            if (parseInt(ieVersion) > 10) return true;

            return false;
        }

        function hashStr(str) {
            var hash = 0;
            var i;
            var chr;
            var len;

            if (str.length === 0) {
                return hash;
            }
            for (i = 0, len = str.length; i < len; i++) {
                chr = str.charCodeAt(i);
                hash = ((hash << 5) - hash) + chr;
                // Convert to 32bit integer
                hash |= 0;
            }

            return Math.abs(hash);
        }
    })();
</script>

        (function() {

                    document.write(scriptTag);
                }
            }
        })();

<script>
    (function() {
        window.beacon('info', ['js_downloaded']);

        var params = window.location.search;

        if (!window.config || !window.angular || !window.main) {

            // remoteconfig experiment flag
            if(true) {
                // if 'prevent_reload' flag is in the URL, we'll fallback.
                if (params.indexOf('prevent_reload') > -1) {
                    return window.fallback('second_script_load_fail', {
                        config: Boolean(window.config),
                        framework: Boolean(window.angular),
                        main: Boolean(window.main)
                    });
                }
                else {
                    // else we'll reload the page from start and append 'prevent_reload' url param to prevent looping
                    window.beacon('info', ['recover_after_script_load_fail'], {
                        config: Boolean(window.config),
                        framework: Boolean(window.angular),
                        main: Boolean(window.main)
                    });

                    window.location = 'https://' + window.location.host +
                                window.location.pathname +
                                params + '&prevent_reload=1' +
                                window.location.hash;
                }
            }
            else {
                return window.fallback('script_load_failed', {
                    config: Boolean(window.config),
                    framework: Boolean(window.angular),
                    main: Boolean(window.main)
                });
            }
        }

        // event to measure successful reloading.
        if (params.indexOf('prevent_reload') > -1) {
            window.beacon('info', ['success_recover_script_load_fail']);
        }

        // default bootstrap timeout
        var timeout = 0;

        // determine if test timeout should be used instead
        if (Math.floor(Math.random() * 100) < 50) {
            timeout = 15;
        }

        window.beacon(
            'info',
            [ 'bootstrap_timeout_setting' ],
            { timeout: timeout, throttle: 50 },
            true
        );

        setTimeout(function() {
            if (!window.bootstrap) {
                return window.fallback('bootstrap_failed');
            }
        }, timeout);
    })();
</script>

<script>
    (function() {

        (function() {
            if (!window.meta || !window.meta.requestTime) return;

            var initialClientTime = new Date().getTime();
            var reqElapsed;

            if (window.enablePerformance) {
                var timing = window.performance.timing;
                reqElapsed = initialClientTime - timing.requestStart;
            }
            else {
                //guess how long it took
                reqElapsed = 500;
            }

            var initialLogTime = window.meta.requestTime + reqElapsed;

            window.logOffset = initialLogTime - initialClientTime;
        })();

        window.beaconQueue = [];

        window.beacon = function(level, events, payload, force, synchronous) {

            // Set up payload

            payload = payload || {};

            payload.event = events.join('|');
            payload.state = 'pre_bootstrap';
            payload.level = level;
            payload.token = 'EC-09B27083D05099223';
            payload.pageID = window.meta && window.meta.pageID;
            payload.timestamp = window.logOffset ?
                new Date(window.logOffset + Date.now()).toString() :
                new Date();

            if (window.enablePerformance) {
                var performance = window.performance;
                var timing      = window.performance.timing || {};

                if (window.clientStartTime) {
                    payload.client_elapsed = parseInt(performance.now() - window.clientStartTime);
                }

                if (timing.connectEnd && timing.navigationStart) {
                    payload.req_elapsed = parseInt(performance.now() - (timing.connectEnd - timing.navigationStart));
                }
            }

            if (!force && level !== 'error' && level !== 'warn') {
                return beaconQueue.push(payload);
            }


            if (window.console && window.console.log) {
                console.log(payload.event, payload);
            }

            // Build URL

            var url   = 'https://www.sandbox.paypal.com/xoplatform/logger/api/log?';
            var query = [];

            for (var prop in payload) {
                query.push(encodeURIComponent(prop) + '=' + encodeURIComponent(payload[prop]));
            }

            url += query.join('&');

            // Set up request
            var req = new XMLHttpRequest();
            req.open('GET', url, !Boolean(synchronous));
            req.send(null);
        };

        window.fallback = function(reason, payload) {
            // Redirect to the error page
            function redirectToError() {
                return window.location = '/webapps/hermes/error';
            }

            // Fallback whitelist experiment: if error reason is not in the whitelist and passes the throttle, go to error page instead
            if (
                10 &&
                !~('windowload_timed_out,bootstrap_failed,buyer_ineligible,transaction_ineligible,ui_unhandled_response_status_404,ul_load_timeout,ui_unhandled_api_error,gce_not_supported,UNSUPPORTED_CUP_SECURECARD,INVALID_IBAN_CODE,MANDATE_METHOD_NOT_ELIGIBLE,SEPA_ACCEPT_CONTINGENCY,ROUTING_NUMBER_NOT_SUPPORTED,fallback_merchant_BA_nocards'.split(',')).indexOf(reason)
            ) {
                if ((Math.random() * 100) < 10) {
                    window.beacon('error', ['fallback_reason_not_whitelisted_treatment'], {reason: reason});

                    return redirectToError();
                } else {
                    window.beacon('error', ['fallback_reason_not_whitelisted_control'], {reason: reason});
                }
            }

            // Determine if we need to make an exception to the fallbacks based on the merchant ID, or as an alternative the country
                var exceptions = {
    "K5GPWSS6GRSTC": [
        "windowload_timed_out"
    ],
    "H2TCH5BL3VBH4": [
        "windowload_timed_out"
    ],
    "BR": [
        "windowload_timed_out"
    ]
};
                var country = 'US';
                var merchantId = 'VSF5E2W5RFWVU';
                var isMobile = ;

                // If we have a valid merchant Id
                if (merchantId.length > 1) {
                    // and merchant Id is in the exceptions list
                    if (exceptions[merchantId]) {
                        if (exceptions[merchantId].indexOf(reason) === -1) {
                            window.beacon('error', ['fallback_to_error_page'], {reason: reason});
                            return redirectToError();
                        }

                        window.beacon('error', ['fallback_ignored'], {reason: reason});
                        return;
                    }
                } else {
                    // If it's a mobile device and the country is in the exceptions list
                    if (isMobile && exceptions[country]) {

                        if (exceptions[country].indexOf(reason) === -1) {
                            window.beacon('error', ['fallback_to_error_page'], {reason: reason});
                            return redirectToError();
                        }

                        window.beacon('error', ['fallback_ignored'], {reason: reason});
                        return;
                    }
                }

            window.fallback = function() {};

            payload = payload || {};
            payload.reason = reason;

            window.beacon('error', [reason, 'fallback', 'fallback_reason_' + reason], payload);

            setTimeout(function() {
                if (~window.location.hostname.indexOf('localhost')) {
                    return console.log('Fallback inhibited on localhost');
                }

                window.onbeforeunload = function() {};
                window.location = '' + meta.fallbackURL + '&token=EC-09B27083D05099223&fallback=1&reason=' + reason;
            }, 500);
        };

        function isPaymentRequestAPISupported() {
            var currentVersionMatch = navigator.userAgent.match(/Chrome\/([0-9]+)\./i);
            return window.navigator.vendor === 'Google Inc.'
                    && 'PaymentRequest' in window
                    && navigator.userAgent.match(/Android/i)
                    && currentVersionMatch
                    && Number(currentVersionMatch[1]) >= 58;
        }

        // Create PaymentRequest object
        function createPaymentRequest() {
            var supportedInstruments = [
                {
                    supportedMethods: ['https://android.com/pay'],
                    data: {
                        minGooglePlayServicesVersion: '10400000',
                        paymentMethodTokenizationParameters: {
                            tokenizationType: 'GATEWAY_TOKEN',
                            parameters: {
                                gateway: 'paypal'
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            ];
            var details = {
                // Payment request requires an amount. Hardcode the value for now.
                total: {label: 'Checkout', amount: {currency: 'USD', value: '1.00'}}
            };

            var options = {};
            return new PaymentRequest(supportedInstruments, details, options);  // eslint-disable-line no-undef
        }

        if (isPaymentRequestAPISupported()) {
            try {
                window.appPaymentRequest = createPaymentRequest();
            } catch(e) {
                window.beacon('error', ['create_payment_request_error'], {
                    name: e && e.name,
                    msg: e && e.message
                });
            }
        }

        // Experimental setting for window load timeout.
        var wl_throttle = 50;
        var wl_testTimeout = 50000;
        var timeout = (Math.floor(Math.random() * 100) < wl_throttle) ? wl_testTimeout : 20000;
        window.beacon('info', ['windowload_timeout_setting'], {'timeout': timeout, 'throttle': wl_throttle}, true);
        var windowLoadTimeout = setTimeout(function() {
            if (!window.bootstrap) {
                return window.fallback('windowload_timed_out');
            }
        }, timeout);

        window.onload = function() {
            clearTimeout(windowLoadTimeout);
        };

        // Log beforeunload event to track of number of users leaving the page before app gets loaded.
        window.onbeforeunload = function() {
            clearTimeout(windowLoadTimeout);
            window.beacon('info', ['pre_bootstrap_window_beforeunload'], {'timeout': timeout, 'throttle': wl_throttle},
                    true, true);
        };

        var windowErrorCache = [];

        window.onerror = function(message, file, line, col, err) {
            message = message && (message.stack || message).toString();

            if (!~windowErrorCache.indexOf(message)) {
                windowErrorCache.push(message);
                beacon('error', ['pre_window_error'], {
                    message: message,
                    file: file && file.toString(),
                    line: line && line.toString(),
                    col: col && col.toString(),
                    stack: err && (err.stack || err).toString()
                });
            }
        };

        window.scripterror = function(event) {
            window.beacon('error', ['script_error'], {
                script: event.target.attributes.src.value
            });
        };

        window.beacon('info', ['pre_bootstrap']);

    })();
</script>

<script>
    (function() {
        var tealeaf;
        // start dynamic script insertion as soon as possible
            tealeaf = {
    "throttle": "5",
    "captureMode": "domcap",
    "scriptSrcPattern": "https://www.paypalobjects.com/js/xo/tealeaf-hermes-prod-02_%.min.js"
};
        if (!tealeaf) {
            return;
        }

        var domcap = 'domcap', classic = 'classic';

        var throttleValue;

        var override = getOverride();
        if (override) {
            window.beacon('info', ['tealeaf_override']);
            throttleValue = -Infinity;
            tealeaf.captureMode = override;
        }
        else {
            throttleValue = hashStr(window.meta.token) % 100;
        }


        if (tealeaf.captureMode !== domcap && tealeaf.captureMode !== classic) {
            window.beacon('info', ['tealeaf_not_enabled'], { reason: 'not_configured' });
            return;
        }

        if (!tealeaf.throttle || throttleValue > parseInt(tealeaf.throttle)) {
            window.beacon('info', ['tealeaf_not_enabled'], { reason: 'throttle' });
            return;
        }

        try {
            var captureMode = tealeaf.captureMode === domcap && validBrowser() ?
                domcap : classic;

            window.beacon('info', ['tealeaf_enabled'], { captureMode: captureMode });

            var script = document.createElement('script');
            script.src = getSrc(captureMode);
            // block execution but not parsing
            // tealeaf needs to be included before 'onload' happens
            script.async = false;
            script.onerror = window.scripterror;
            document.head.appendChild(script);
        }
        catch (e) {
            window.beacon('error', ['tealeaf_include_failed'], {
                name: e && e.name,
                msg: e && e.message
            });
        }

        function getOverride() {
            if (window.location.search.indexOf('tealeaf_domcap_override') !== -1) return domcap;
            if (window.location.search.indexOf('tealeaf_classic_override') !== -1) return classic;
        }

        function getSrc(captureMode) {
            return tealeaf.scriptSrcPattern.replace('%', captureMode);
        }

        function validBrowser() {
            var ieVersion = new Function("/*@cc_on return @_jscript_version; @*/")();

            if (!ieVersion) return true;

            if (parseInt(ieVersion) > 10) return true;

            return false;
        }

        function hashStr(str) {
            var hash = 0;
            var i;
            var chr;
            var len;

            if (str.length === 0) {
                return hash;
            }
            for (i = 0, len = str.length; i < len; i++) {
                chr = str.charCodeAt(i);
                hash = ((hash << 5) - hash) + chr;
                // Convert to 32bit integer
                hash |= 0;
            }

            return Math.abs(hash);
        }
    })();
</script>

    <script>
        (function() {
            if (window.name && window.name.indexOf('xcomponent') === 0) {
                var version = window.name.split('__')[2].replace(/_/g, '.');
                if (version.match(/^[0-9a-zA-Z\.]+$/)) {

                    if (version === '4' || version === 'latest') {
                        version = '';
                    }

                    var scriptTag = '<scr' + 'ipt src="https://www.paypalobjects.com/api/checkout' + (version ? ('.' + version) : '') + '.js" onerror="scripterror(event)" data-paypal-checkout data-no-bridge data-state="ppxo_checkout"></scr' + 'ipt>';
                    document.write(scriptTag);
                }
            }
        })();
    </script>

<script>
    (function() {
        window.beacon('info', ['js_downloaded']);

        var params = window.location.search;

        if (!window.config || !window.angular || !window.main) {

            // remoteconfig experiment flag
            if(true) {
                // if 'prevent_reload' flag is in the URL, we'll fallback.
                if (params.indexOf('prevent_reload') > -1) {
                    return window.fallback('second_script_load_fail', {
                        config: Boolean(window.config),
                        framework: Boolean(window.angular),
                        main: Boolean(window.main)
                    });
                }
                else {
                    // else we'll reload the page from start and append 'prevent_reload' url param to prevent looping
                    window.beacon('info', ['recover_after_script_load_fail'], {
                        config: Boolean(window.config),
                        framework: Boolean(window.angular),
                        main: Boolean(window.main)
                    });

                    window.location = 'https://' + window.location.host +
                                window.location.pathname +
                                params + '&prevent_reload=1' +
                                window.location.hash;
                }
            }
            else {
                return window.fallback('script_load_failed', {
                    config: Boolean(window.config),
                    framework: Boolean(window.angular),
                    main: Boolean(window.main)
                });
            }
        }

        // event to measure successful reloading.
        if (params.indexOf('prevent_reload') > -1) {
            window.beacon('info', ['success_recover_script_load_fail']);
        }

        // default bootstrap timeout
        var timeout = 0;

        // determine if test timeout should be used instead
        if (Math.floor(Math.random() * 100) < 50) {
            timeout = 15;
        }

        window.beacon(
            'info',
            [ 'bootstrap_timeout_setting' ],
            { timeout: timeout, throttle: 50 },
            true
        );

        setTimeout(function() {
            if (!window.bootstrap) {
                return window.fallback('bootstrap_failed');
            }
        }, timeout);
    })();
</script>
